1c:I[9539,["5034","static/chunks/5034-5887c1fdc6f0a5a7.js","4921","static/chunks/4921-980f076695cdb8cd.js","9749","static/chunks/9749-aae10d34a9ebd952.js","3026","static/chunks/3026-2c14a3fc951b4932.js","1373","static/chunks/app/franchises/%5Bslug%5D/page-9c76bb68ebdca3ff.js"],"default"]
1d:T442,The Avarona family was once amongst the most powerful in the Realm. During the First Great War, this family refused to join the Legions of Light, believing they would lose the battle. After the defeat of the Dark Four, the traitorous Avaronas were stripped of their station and banished from Leandorr. Since that time, the Avaronas have worked to regain their influence, leading them to align now with the Legion of Arethyr. Lady Avarona is the youngest daughter of the family, and the cruelest by far. While the rest of the family are focused on reestablishing their power, Lady Avarona is driven purely by a hunger to take revenge on those who disgraced her family.

Note: The Lady Avarona figure will come with both the soft goods loin piece shown as well as a standard, plastic loin piece part.

Mythic Legions is an expansive fantasy world of action figures created by the award winning Four Horsemen Studios. All figures are highly articulated and stand in the 6 inch scale.
